# Latn-script languages

Selected character-set databases (CLDR, Latin Plus) juxtaposed next to Rosetta’s Langs DB. When comparing, characters that are included in “Rosetta (base)” are marked grey, any additional characters are marked red. Only “base” fields are compared. The third column indicates whether the field is “todo” (grey) or “done” (green). In case of CLDR, grey refers to draft having been “contributed”.

## Eastern Abnaki (aaq)

 <tr><th>rstt (base):</th><td>a b c d e f g h i j k l m n o p q r s t u v w x y z ô</td><td class='todo'></td></tr>
 </table>
